md-inline=\"strong\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">Flask</span></strong>是一个使用Python编写的轻量级Web应用框架。其WSGI</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">工具箱采用Werkzeug，模板引擎则使用Jinja2。</span></span></p>\n<p SimSun;\"><span md-inline=\"strong\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">SSTI</span></strong>(Server-Side Template</span> <span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">Injection)，即服务端模板注入攻击。通过与服务端模板的输入输出交互，在过滤不严格的情况下，构造恶意输入数据，从而达到读取文件或者</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">getshell的目的。</span></span></p>\n<p Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">jinja2 语法</span></h3>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">在jinja2中，存在三种语法：</span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre class=\"code-snippet__js\">控制结构&#160;{%&#160;%}\n变量取值&#160;{{&#160;}}\n注释&#160;{#&#160;#}</pre>\n</section>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">jinja2模板中使用{{ }}</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">语法表示一个变量，它是一种特殊的占位符。当利用jinja2进行渲染的时候，它会把这些特殊的占位符进行填充/替换，jinja2</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">支持Python中所有的Python数据类型比如列表、字段、对象等。jinja2</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">中的过滤器可以理解为是jinja2里面的内置函数和字符串处理函数。</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">被两个括号包裹的内容会输出其表达式的值。</span></span></p>\n<h3 cid=\"n17\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.5em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">沙箱绕过</span></h3>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-140019-1598860510.jpeg\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em SimSun;\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">jinja2的Python</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">模板解释器在构建的时候考虑到了安全问题，删除了大部分敏感函数，相当于构建了一个沙箱环境。但是一些内置函数和属性还是依然可以使用，而</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">Flask的SSTI</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">就是利用这些内置函数和属性相互组建来达到调用函数的目的，从而绕过沙箱。</span></span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">函数和属性解析:</strong></span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre data-lang=\"markdown\" style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em 1em 1em 0px;max-width: 1000%;overflow-x: auto;white-space: normal;-webkit-box-flex: 1;flex: 1 1 0%;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-size: 14px;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important\">__class__&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;返回调用的参数类型\n__bases__&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;返回基类列表\n__mro__&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;此属性是在方法解析期间寻找基类时的参考类元组\n__subclasses__()&#160;&#160;返回子类的列表\n__globals__&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;以字典的形式返回函数所在的全局命名空间所定义的全局变量&#160;与&#160;func_globals&#160;等价\n__builtins__&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;内建模块的引用，在任何地方都是可见的(包括全局)，每个&#160;Python&#160;脚本都会自动加载，这个模块包括了很多强大的&#160;built-in&#160;函数，例如eval,&#160;exec,&#160;open等等</pre>\n</section>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">发现子类型有很多，在这里我们需要找到内建模块中含有eval或者open</span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: Group，对象管理组织。是一个国际化的、开放成员的、非盈利性的计算机行业标准协会，该协会成立于1989年，其职责是为应用开发提供一个公共框架，制订工业指南和对象管理规范，加快对象技术的发展。OMG还制定了广为人知的中间件标准CommonObject Request Broker Architecture (CORBA)</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n8\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">接口描述语言（或者叫接口定义语言，Interface Definition Language）</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p cid=\"n23\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: </span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p cid=\"n25\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IIOP标准（网络ORB交换协议， Internet Inter ORB Protocol）</span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p cid=\"n27\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n28\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IDL</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n29\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IDL（Interface Definition Language）接口定义语言，它主要用于描述软件组件的应用程序编程接口的一种规范语言。它完成了与各种编程语言（Ada、C、C++、Smalltalk、Java等）无关的映射，可以将IDL翻译成各种语言，从而实现了不同语言之间的通信，这样就保证了跨语言跨环境的远程对象调用。</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n32\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n33\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">ORB</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n34\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">ORB（Object Request Broker）对象请求代理，是建立Client/Server关系的中间件。使用ORB，一个客户可以很简单地使用服务器对象的方法而不论服务器是在同一机器上还是通过一个网络访问。ORB 截获调用然后负责找到一个对象实现这个请求，传递参数和方法，最后返回结果。客户不用知道对象在哪里，是什么语言实现的，他的操作系统以及其他和对象接口无关的东西。</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n35\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n36\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">ORBD</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n37\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">ORBD（The Object Request Broker Daemon）对象请求代理守护程序，当</span><span md-inline=\"code\" spellcheck=\"false\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\"><code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-family: var(--monospace);vertical-align: initial;border: 1px solid rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding: 0px 2px;font-size: 0.9em\">orbd</code></span><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">启动时，它还会启动一个命名服务。ORBD用于使客户端能够透明地定位和调用CORBA环境中服务器上的持久对象。</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n38\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n40\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IOR</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n41\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IOR（Interoperable Object Reference）互操作对象引用，是CORBA或RMI-IIOP中联系方式客户端应用程序用于与CORBA对象进行通信的，用于唯一标识和定位远程CORBA服务器上的对象。IOR是以特定方式编码的文本字符串，它包含足够的信息以允许：</span></p>\n<ul cid=\"n42\" mdtype=\"list\" data-mark=\"-\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;padding-left: 30px;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;white-space: normal\" class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p cid=\"n44\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">定向到正确服务器的请求（主机，端口号）</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p cid=\"n46\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">要定位或创建的对象（类名，实例数据）</span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p cid=\"n47\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n48\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">GIOP</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n49\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">GIOP（General Inter-ORB Protocol）通用对象请求代理间通信协议，提供了一个标准传输语法（低层数据表示方法）和ORB之间通信的信息格式集。GIOP只能用在ORB与ORB之间，而且，只能在符合理想条件的面向连接传输协议中使用。它不需要使用更高一层的RPC机制。</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n50\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n52\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IIOP</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n53\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">IIOP（Internet Inter-ORB Protocol）网络对象代理间通信协议，指出如何通过TCP/IP连接交换GIOP信息。它是TCP/IP环境下基本的inter-ORB协议（GIOP的具体实现），最普遍的传输层。</span> <span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">GIOP 不基于任何特别的网络协议，OMG 在最广泛使用的通信传输平台 -- TCP/IP 上标准化 GIOP，GIOP 加 TCP/IP 等于 IIOP</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n54\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n56\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">POA</span></h2>\n<p cid=\"n57\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">POA（Portable Object Adapter）便携式对象适配器，对象适配器是一种机制，服务器端可以创建servant关联的对象引用，并且使用正确的对象引用连接为请求提供服务。</span></p>\n<p cid=\"n58\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n60\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">网络协议栈模型</span></h2>\n<h2 cid=\"n64\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;orphans: 4;font-size: 1.75em;margin-top: 1rem;margin-bottom: 1rem;position: relative;line-height: 1.225;cursor: text;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\"><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image-20200827150740891.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image-20200827150740891.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image-20200827150740891.png\" alt=\"image-20200827150740891.png\"/></a></span></h2>\n<h2 cid=\"n64\" mdtype=\"heading\" class=\"md-end-block md-heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: &#39;Open Sans&#39;, &#39;Clear Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif\">CORBA通信流程</h2>\n<p cid=\"n65\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" class=\"md-end-block md-p\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;line-height: inherit;orphans: 4;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative;color: rgb(51, 51, border-box\">CORBA还可以简单分为三个部分：</span></p>\n<ul cid=\"n66\" mdtype=\"list\" data-mark=\"-\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;margin-top: 0.8em;margin-bottom: 0.8em;padding-left: 30px;position: 0.5rem;white-space: pre-wrap;position: relative\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">naming service(ORBD)</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p cid=\"n70\" mdtype=\"paragraph\" Sans&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px\"><span md-inline=\"plain\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\">以前，Java 程序员必须针对分布式编程解决方案在 RMI 和 CORBA/IIOP (Java IDL) 之间进行选择。现在，通过遵循一些限制（请参阅</span><span md-inline=\"link\" class=\"md-meta-i-c  md-link\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box\"><a spellcheck=\"false\" 11:03:01","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 11:03:01","title":"​GODNSLOG | 开源一个新鲜的DNSLOG","link":"https://www.secpulse.com/?p=140063","description":"<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/banner.png\" title=\"banner.png\" alt=\"banner.png\"/></p>\n<h2>背景动机</h2>\n<section>之前有一段工作是跟漏扫相关的，在开发漏扫时有DNSLOG这么一个需求，当时考虑到时间成本没有自己做。虽然现有市面上DNSLOG不少，我还是重复造了一个轮子， 有多个原因。现有的开源DNSLOG体验没有一些知名闭源的DNSLOG平台好，站在甲方的立场自建的服务总归是比使用公共服务好一些，毕竟没有多少人愿意把自己的漏洞情况让第三方知道。此外现有DNSLOG平台IP已经上了威胁情报名单，在不少环境这些IP直接就被干掉了，特别是在公有云环境下。所以<strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial\">甲方自建DNSLOG服务非常有必要</strong>。现有的开源DNSLOG python项目居多，也有个别golang的，<strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial\">在我看来安全开发的技术架构方向一定是微服务化、SaaS化</strong>，python程序封装成docker体积确实有点大。刚好最近看了一点vue，想写个东西练练手，就把这个事情捡起来。GODNSLOG前端是套了ant design vue pro，后端用golang开发。</section>\n<p><br/></p>\n<h2>功能特性 &#38; 用法简介</h2>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<section><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 17px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">1. DNSLOG</strong></span></section>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<section>每个用户分配一个唯一的三级域名，该域名或其子域名的所有解析记录均会被记录。<br/>请求记录超过设置的最长时间会被自动清理，自动清理时间设置范围是1-48小时</section>\n<pre><code>dig `/sbin/ifconfig eth0|grep inet|grep -v 127.0.0.1|grep -v inet6|awk &#39;{print $2}&#39;|tr -d &#34;addr:&#34;`.ktqlujjpgc4j.godns.vip<br/></code></pre>\n<p>系统生成域名为{$variable}.ktqlujjpgc4j.godns.vip，其中ktqlujjpgc4j是用户唯一shortId，{$variable}为用户自定义变量</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/dnslog-1024x415.png\" title=\"dnslog-1024x415.png\" alt=\"dnslog.png\"/></p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;padding: 0px;clear: both;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;font-family: Helvetica, arial, freesans, clean, sans-serif;font-size: 14px;text-align: start\"><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 17px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">2. HTTPLOG</strong></span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<section>HTTPLOG也需要用到唯一分配的域名，HTTPLOG地址格式如下，所有访问以下地址的请求会被记录。<br/>请求记录超过设置的最长时间会被自动清理，自动清理时间设置范围是1-48小时</section>\n<pre><code>curl http://100.100.100.100/log/ktqlujjpgc4j/`/sbin/ifconfig eth0|grep inet|grep -v 127.0.0.1|grep -v inet6|awk &#39;{print $2}&#39;|tr -d &#34;addr:&#34;`<br/></code></pre>\n<p>除了只能用DNSLOG检测的情况，HTTPLOG都比DNSLOG好用一些，在内网环境中配合主动推送可以让检出更有效率，代码也相对简单一些。</p>\n<p><br/></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/httplog-2-1024x240.png\" title=\"httplog-2-1024x240.png\" alt=\"httplog-2.png\"/></p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;padding: 0px;clear: both;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;font-family: Helvetica, arial, freesans, clean, sans-serif;font-size: 14px;text-align: start\"><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 17px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">3. DNS Rebinding</strong></span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<section>这是河马安全团队的另一位成员提的需求。目前的策略是每次请求随机返回一个配置列表中的IP，后面再升级一些高级策略</section>\n<p><br/></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/rebind-setting-1024x433.png\" title=\"rebind-setting-1024x433.png\" alt=\"rebind-setting.png\"/></p>\n<p>注:一些本地DNS即时收到TTL=0的DNS也依然会缓存，比如说腾讯云会缓存1分钟</p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 0px;clear: both\"><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 17px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">4. 多用户</strong></span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;text-indent: 2em\">两级用户，内置用户为管理员，管理员可以新建、修改、删除普通用户。</span><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;text-indent: 2em\">普通用户拥有除用户管理功能之外的所有功能</span></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/user-admin-1024x303.png\" title=\"user-admin-1024x303.png\" alt=\"user-admin.png\"/></p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;padding: 0px;clear: both;border-width: 0px;border-style: initial;border-color: initial;font-family: Helvetica, arial, freesans, clean, sans-serif;font-size: 14px;text-align: start\"><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 17px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">5. 主动推送</strong></span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<section>这个功能是给内网部署时设计的，我们在检测是否记录时一般是用api查询的，这里需要有个等待机制。跟这种pull的方式对应的就是push方式，在配置/系统模块配置。主动推送比较适合在内网使用，在内网环境中HTTPLOG+主动推送</section>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 0px;clear: both\"><span style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 17px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">6. 支持API调用</strong></span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p>传统的pull api模式，客户端通过token+api的方式查询DNS/HTTP记录，这里我改进了一下，一般的DNSLOG平台token直接在URL中传递不是很安全，稍微改进了一下，用hash校验替代了token校验。GODNSLOG将支持精准查询和模糊查询两种方式</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/api-token3-1024x209.png\" title=\"api-token3-1024x209.png\" alt=\"api-token3.png\"/></p>\n<h2>安装部署</h2>\n<p>docker一键部署，推荐http前面套个nginx可以套SSL证书</p>\n<p>需求：一个域名、用户独立IP的主机.</p>\n<p><br/></p>\n<section><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">1.修改域名DNS服务器，使用独立主机IP作为域名的DNS服务器</strong></section>\n<section><span style=\"font-size: 14px\">修改生效需要数小时到48小时，需要等全球DNS都刷新。修改完成之后所有的*.godnslog.com均会指向100.100.100.100</span></section>\n<p>注：如果在内网环境中使用，域名也不是一定要注册的，在内网DNS中配置一个私有域名即可</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-size: 16px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">2. 安装docker环境，并启动实例</strong></span></p>\n<pre><code>curl -s https://get.docker.com/ | sudo sh<br/>systemctl enable docker<br/>systemctl start docker<br/>docker pull sort/godnslog:version-0.3.0<br/>docker run -d --name=godnslog -p8080:8080 -p53:53/udp sort/godnslog:version-0.3.0 -domain=godnslog.com -4 100.100.100.100<br/></code></pre>\n<p>godnslog默认使用sqlite数据库，考虑到性能建议使用外部mysql.<br/>命令行参数可以用以下命令查看</p>\n<pre><code>docker run --rm --it sort/godnslog:version-0.3.0 --help</code></pre>\n<p>注: 此处version-0.3.0为当前版本，后续可能会改动，请使用最新版本</p>\n<p>mysql DSN格式:&#160;<a href=\"https://github.com/go-sql-driver/mysql/#dsn-data-source-name\">https://github.com/go-sql-driver/mysql/#dsn-data-source-name</a></p>\n<p>sqlite DSN格式:&#160;<a href=\"https://github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3#dsn-examples\">https://github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3#dsn-examples</a></p>\n<p>关于持久化，使用外部mysql时数据就是持久化的，sqlite要支持持久化需要通过docker -v参数将宿主机上的文件映射为sqlite数据库文件，否则重启docker后数据会丢失</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-size: 16px\"><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">3. 配置</strong></span></p>\n<p><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">3.1 安装nginx</strong></p>\n<pre><code>yum install nginx<br/>systemctl start nginx<br/>systemctl enable nginx<br/></code></pre>\n<p><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">3.2 配置并重启nginx</strong></p>\n<pre><code>server {<br/> &#160; &#160;listen &#160; &#160; &#160; 80 default_server;<br/> &#160; &#160;server_name &#160;www.godnslog.com *.godnslog.com;<br/><br/> &#160; &#160;# Load configuration files for the default server block.<br/> &#160; &#160;access_log /var/log/nginx/www.godnslog.com.access.log;<br/> &#160; &#160;error_log /var/log/nginx/www.godnslog.com.error.log;<br/><br/> &#160; &#160;proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For &#160;$proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;<br/> &#160; &#160;proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;<br/> &#160; &#160;proxy_set_header Host &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160; $host;<br/> &#160; &#160;proxy_set_header X-Real-IP &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160;$remote_addr;<br/><br/> &#160; &#160;location / {<br/> &#160; &#160; &#160; &#160;proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:8080;<br/> &#160; &#160;}<br/>}<br/></code></pre>\n<p><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">3.3 配置防火墙开放UDP:53，TCP:80端口</strong></p>\n<p><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\">3.4 登录配置用户</strong></p>\n<section>内置管理员用户名为admin,密码为password，安装完成后请尽快修改管理员密码。<br/>登录管理员帐户后可以在配置/用户中管理用户</section>\n<p><br/></p>\n<h2>演示网站</h2>\n<p>演示网站: <a href=\"https://www.godns.vip\">https://www.godns.vip</a></p>\n<p>测试账号：</p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 0px;clear: both\">test1/test123456</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 0px;clear: both\">test2/test123456</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 演示网站仅提供演示功能，不要用在实际环境，随时可能重启升级!</strong></p>\n<p><strong style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px\"><br/></strong></p>\n<section>演示网站本来是申请了godnslog.com，这里吐槽下腾讯云，不支持自定义DNS host也就罢了，坑爹的修改DNS服务器IP还失败了。被迫昨晚又在阿里云申请了gons.vip。推荐在阿里云或者cheapname申请域名。</section>\n<p><br/></p>\n<h2>结语</h2>\n<section></section>\n<section>\n<p>GODNSLOG设计实现很大程度借鉴了ceye.io，关于DNSLOG的技巧<a
